&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Added a network sandbox proxy with policy enforcement to better control outbound network access. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3754844145&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8442&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8442/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8442&quot;&gt;#8442&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Introduced the first phase of connectors support via the app server and MCP integration, including new config/docs updates. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3841758895&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9667&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9667/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9667&quot;&gt;#9667&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Shipped collaboration mode as beta in the TUI, with a clearer plan → execute handoff and simplified mode selection (Coding vs Plan). (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3843432600&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9690&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9690/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9690&quot;&gt;#9690&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3844493018&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9712&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9712/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9712&quot;&gt;#9712&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3849957804&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9802&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9802/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9802&quot;&gt;#9802&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3852399329&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9834&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9834/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9834&quot;&gt;#9834&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Added ephemeral threads and improved collaboration tool provenance metadata for spawned threads. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3847420254&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9765&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9765/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9765&quot;&gt;#9765&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3847566538&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9769&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9769/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9769&quot;&gt;#9769&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;

&lt;h2&gt;Bug Fixes&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Fixed exec policy parsing for multiline quoted arguments. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3836034142&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9565&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9565/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9565&quot;&gt;#9565&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;

(&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3836747853&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9590&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9590/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9590&quot;&gt;#9590&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Improved resume reliability by handling out-of-order events and prompting for the working directory when it differs. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3831833721&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9512&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9512/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9512&quot;&gt;#9512&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3845460654&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9731&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9731/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9731&quot;&gt;#9731&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;

(&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3840001499&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9630&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9630/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9630&quot;&gt;#9630&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;

&lt;/ul&gt;</content:encoded></item><item><title>Team Config for shared configuration</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2026-01-23-mdx</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2026-01-23-mdx</guid><description>Team Config for shared configuration</description><pubDate>Fri, 23 Jan 2026 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded># Team Config for shared configuration

Team Config groups the files teams use to standardize Codex across repositories and machines. Use it to share:

- `config.toml` defaults
- `rules/` for command controls outside the sandbox
- `skills/` for reusable workflows

Codex loads these layers from `.codex/` folders in the current working directory, parent folders, and the repo root, plus user (`~/.codex/`) and system (`/etc/codex/`) locations. Higher-precedence locations override lower-precedence ones.

Admins can still enforce constraints with `requirements.toml`, which overrides defaults regardless of location.

Learn more in [Team Config](/codex/team-config).</content:encoded></item><item><title>Custom prompts deprecated</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2026-01-22-mdx</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2026-01-22-mdx</guid><description>Custom prompts deprecated</description><pubDate>Thu, 22 Jan 2026 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded># Custom prompts deprecated

Custom prompts are now deprecated. Use [skills](/codex/skills) for reusable instructions and workflows instead.</content:encoded></item><item><title>Expanded llms.txt coverage</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#developers-2026-01-22-mdx</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#developers-2026-01-22-mdx</guid><description>Expanded llms.txt coverage to include resources, blog posts, cookbook entries, and the developer changelog, with full exports where available.</description><pubDate>Thu, 22 Jan 2026 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded># Expanded llms.txt coverage

## Fixes &amp; improvements
- Expanded llms.txt coverage to include resources, blog posts, cookbook entries, and the developer changelog, with full exports where available.</content:encoded></item><item><title>Codex CLI Release: 0.89.0</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-279171728</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-279171728</guid><description>0.89.0</description><pubDate>Thu, 22 Jan 2026 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded>&lt;h2&gt;New Features&lt;/h2&gt;

&lt;li&gt;Added a &lt;code&gt;/permissions&lt;/code&gt; command with a shorter approval set while keeping &lt;code&gt;/approvals&lt;/code&gt; for compatibility. ## Fixes &amp; improvements
- Added [company knowledge in ChatGPT](https://openai.com/index/introducing-company-knowledge/) compatibility guidance for the `search`/`fetch` tools. [Click here to learn more](/apps-sdk/build/mcp-server#company-knowledge-compatibility).</content:encoded></item><item><title>Codex CLI Release: 0.88.0</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-278754265</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-278754265</guid><description>0.88.0</description><pubDate>Wed, 21 Jan 2026 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded>&lt;h2&gt;New Features&lt;/h2&gt;

&lt;/ul&gt;</content:encoded></item><item><title>Codex CLI Release: 0.87.0</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-277440557</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-277440557</guid><description>0.87.0</description><pubDate>Fri, 16 Jan 2026 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded>&lt;h2&gt;New Features&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;User message metadata (text elements and byte ranges) now round-trips through protocol/app-server/core so UI annotations can survive history rebuilds. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3819645680&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9331&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9331/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9331&quot;&gt;#9331&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Collaboration wait calls can block on multiple IDs in one request, simplifying multi-thread coordination. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3818331608&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9294&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9294/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9294&quot;&gt;#9294&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;User shell commands now run under the user snapshot so aliases and shell config are honored. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3821279349&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9357&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9357/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9357&quot;&gt;#9357&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;The TUI now surfaces approval requests from spawned/unsubscribed threads. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3815136192&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9232&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9232/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9232&quot;&gt;#9232&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Bug Fixes&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Token estimation during compaction is now accurate, improving budgeting during long sessions. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3819877714&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9337&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9337/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9337&quot;&gt;#9337&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;MCP CallToolResult now includes &lt;code&gt;threadId&lt;/code&gt; in both &lt;code&gt;content&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;code&gt;structuredContent&lt;/code&gt;, and returns a defined output schema for compatibility. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3819882393&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9338&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9338/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9338&quot;&gt;#9338&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;The TUI “Worked for” separator only appears after actual work has occurred. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3795691757&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8958&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8958/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8958&quot;&gt;#8958&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Piped non-PTY commands no longer hang waiting on stdin. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3822258861&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9369&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9369/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9369&quot;&gt;#9369&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Documentation&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;MCP interface docs updated to reflect structured output schema and &lt;code&gt;threadId&lt;/code&gt; behavior. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3819882393&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9338&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9338/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9338&quot;&gt;#9338&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Chores&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Windows builds enable the PowerShell UTF-8 feature by default. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3811768145&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9195&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9195/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9195&quot;&gt;#9195&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;

&lt;/ul&gt;</content:encoded></item><item><title>Codex CLI Release: 0.86.0</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-277242575</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-277242575</guid><description>0.86.0</description><pubDate>Fri, 16 Jan 2026 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded>&lt;h2&gt;New Features&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Skill metadata can now be defined in &lt;code&gt;SKILL.toml&lt;/code&gt; (names, descriptions, icons, brand color, default prompt) and surfaced in the app server and TUI (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3806601125&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9125&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9125/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9125&quot;&gt;#9125&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Clients can explicitly disable web search and signal eligibility via a header to align with server-side rollout controls (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3815581879&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9249&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9249/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9249&quot;&gt;#9249&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Bug Fixes&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Accepting an MCP elicitation now sends an empty JSON payload instead of null to satisfy servers expecting content (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3812090115&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9196&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9196/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9196&quot;&gt;#9196&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Input prompt placeholder styling is back to non-italic to avoid terminal rendering issues (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3818679832&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9307&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9307/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9307&quot;&gt;#9307&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Empty paste events no longer trigger clipboard image reads (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3819198524&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9318&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9318/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9318&quot;&gt;#9318&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Unified exec cleans up background processes to prevent late End events after listeners stop (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3818563756&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9304&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9304/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9304&quot;&gt;#9304&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Chores&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Refresh the orchestrator prompt to improve internal routing behavior (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3818481765&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9301&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9301/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9301&quot;&gt;#9301&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Reduce noisy &lt;code&gt;needs_follow_up&lt;/code&gt; error logging (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3817101621&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9272&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9272/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9272&quot;&gt;#9272&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;

&lt;/ul&gt;</content:encoded></item><item><title>Session metadata for tool calls &amp; requestModal template switching</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#apps-sdk-2026-01-15-mdx</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#apps-sdk-2026-01-15-mdx</guid><description>Tool calls now include `_meta[&quot;openai/session&quot;]`, an anonymized conversation id you can use to correlate requests within a ChatGPT session. `window.openai.requestModal({ template })` now supports opening a different registered UI template by passing the template URI from `registerResource`.</description><pubDate>Thu, 15 Jan 2026 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded># Session metadata for tool calls &amp; requestModal template switching

## Fixes &amp; improvements
- Tool calls now include `_meta[&quot;openai/session&quot;]`, an anonymized conversation id you can use to correlate requests within a ChatGPT session.
- `window.openai.requestModal({ template })` now supports opening a different registered UI template by passing the template URI from `registerResource`.</content:encoded></item><item><title>Codex CLI Release: 0.85.0</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-277157618</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-277157618</guid><description>0.85.0</description><pubDate>Thu, 15 Jan 2026 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded>&lt;h2&gt;New Features&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;App-server v2 now emits collaboration tool calls as item events in the turn stream, so clients can render agent coordination in real time. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3814296959&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9213&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9213/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9213&quot;&gt;#9213&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Collaboration tools gained richer agent control: &lt;code&gt;spawn_agent&lt;/code&gt; accepts an agent role preset, and &lt;code&gt;send_input&lt;/code&gt; can optionally interrupt a running agent before delivering the message. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3817182945&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9275&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9275/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9275&quot;&gt;#9275&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3817190211&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9276&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9276/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9276&quot;&gt;#9276&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;code&gt;/models&lt;/code&gt; metadata now includes upgrade migration markdown so clients can display richer guidance when suggesting model upgrades. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3814556680&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9219&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9219/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9219&quot;&gt;#9219&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Bug Fixes&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;[revert] Linux sandboxing now falls back to Landlock-only restrictions when user namespaces are unavailable, and sets &lt;code&gt;no_new_privs&lt;/code&gt; before applying sandbox rules. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3815622638&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9250&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9250/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9250&quot;&gt;#9250&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;code&gt;codex resume --last&lt;/code&gt; now respects the current working directory, with &lt;code&gt;--all&lt;/code&gt; as an explicit override. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3815452164&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9245&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9245/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9245&quot;&gt;#9245&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Stdin prompt decoding now handles BOMs/UTF-16 and provides clearer errors for invalid encodings. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3809421637&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9151&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9151/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9151&quot;&gt;#9151&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;

GPT-5.2-Codex is now available in the API and for users who sign into Codex with the API.

To learn more about using GPT-5.2-Codex check out our [API documentation](https://platform.openai.com/docs/models/gpt-5.2-codex).</content:encoded></item><item><title>Codex CLI Release: 0.81.0</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-276819252</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-276819252</guid><description>0.81.0</description><pubDate>Wed, 14 Jan 2026 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded>&lt;h2&gt;New Features&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Default API model moved to gpt-5.2-codex. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3811171344&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9188&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9188/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9188&quot;&gt;#9188&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;The &lt;code&gt;codex&lt;/code&gt; tool in &lt;code&gt;codex mcp-server&lt;/code&gt; now includes the &lt;code&gt;threadId&lt;/code&gt; in the response so it can be used with the &lt;code&gt;codex-reply&lt;/code&gt; tool, fixing &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3421157113&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/3712&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;issue&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/issues/3712/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/3712&quot;&gt;#3712&lt;/a&gt;. The documentation has been updated at &lt;a href=&quot;https://developers.openai.com/codex/guides/agents-sdk/&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow&quot;&gt;https://developers.openai.com/codex/guides/agents-sdk/&lt;/a&gt;. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3811598073&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9192&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9192/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9192&quot;&gt;#9192&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Headless runs now switch to device-code login automatically so sign-in works without a browser. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3782756626&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8756&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8756/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8756&quot;&gt;#8756&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Linux sandbox can mount paths read-only to better protect files from writes. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3805982528&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9112&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9112/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9112&quot;&gt;#9112&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Support partial tool calls rendering in &lt;code&gt;tui&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Bug Fixes&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Alternate-screen handling now avoids breaking Zellij scrollback and adds a config/flag to control it. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3763567492&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8555&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8555/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8555&quot;&gt;#8555&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Windows correctly prompts before unsafe commands when running with a read-only sandbox policy. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3806353935&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9117&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9117/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9117&quot;&gt;#9117&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Config.toml and rules parsing errors are reported to app-server clients/TUI instead of failing silently. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3811075129&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9182&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9182/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9182&quot;&gt;#9182&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3798794868&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/9011&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/9011/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/9011&quot;&gt;#9011&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Worked around a macOS system-configuration crash in proxy discovery. &lt;/ul&gt;</content:encoded></item><item><title>Codex CLI Release: 0.80.0</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-275597320</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-275597320</guid><description>0.80.0</description><pubDate>Fri, 09 Jan 2026 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded>&lt;h2&gt;New Features&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Add conversation/thread fork endpoints in the protocol and app server so clients can branch a session into a new thread. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3790641311&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8866&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8866/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8866&quot;&gt;#8866&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Expose requirements via &lt;code&gt;requirement/list&lt;/code&gt; so clients can read &lt;code&gt;requirements.toml&lt;/code&gt; and adjust agent-mode UX. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3786881459&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8800&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8800/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8800&quot;&gt;#8800&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Introduce metrics capabilities with additional counters for observability. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3747568183&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8318&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8318/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8318&quot;&gt;#8318&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3793211338&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8910&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8910/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8910&quot;&gt;#8910&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Add elevated sandbox onboarding with prompts for upgrade/degraded mode plus the &lt;code&gt;/elevate-sandbox&lt;/code&gt; command. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3786208551&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8789&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8789/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8789&quot;&gt;#8789&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Allow explicit skill invocations through v2 API user input. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3790565855&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8864&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8864/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8864&quot;&gt;#8864&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Bug Fixes&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Codex CLI subprocesses again inherit env vars like &lt;code&gt;LD_LIBRARY_PATH&lt;/code&gt;/&lt;code&gt;DYLD_LIBRARY_PATH&lt;/code&gt; to avoid runtime issues. As explained in &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3794801480&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8945&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;issue&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/issues/8945/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8945&quot;&gt;#8945&lt;/a&gt;, failure to pass along these environment variables to subprocesses that expect them (notably GPU-related ones), was causing 10x+ performance regressions! Special thanks to &lt;a class=&quot;user-mention notranslate&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;user&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/users/johnzfitch/hovercard&quot; data-octo-click=&quot;hovercard-link-click&quot; data-octo-dimensions=&quot;link_type:self&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/johnzfitch&quot;&gt;@johnzfitch&lt;/a&gt; for the detailed investigation and write-up in &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3794801480&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8945&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;issue&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/issues/8945/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8945&quot;&gt;#8945&lt;/a&gt;. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3795141641&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8951&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8951/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8951&quot;&gt;#8951&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;code&gt;/review &amp;lt;instructions&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt; in TUI/TUI2 now launches the review flow instead of sending plain text. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3788534686&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8823&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8823/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8823&quot;&gt;#8823&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Patch approval “allow this session” now sticks for previously approved files. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3755457608&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8451&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8451/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8451&quot;&gt;#8451&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Model upgrade prompt now appears even if the current model is hidden from the picker. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3786982639&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8802&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8802/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8802&quot;&gt;#8802&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Windows paste handling now supports non-ASCII multiline input reliably. Special thanks to &lt;a class=&quot;user-mention notranslate&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;user&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/users/occurrent/hovercard&quot; data-octo-click=&quot;hovercard-link-click&quot; data-octo-dimensions=&quot;link_type:self&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/occurrent&quot;&gt;@occurrent&lt;/a&gt; laying the groundwork for this fix in &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3727879517&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8021&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8021/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8021&quot;&gt;#8021&lt;/a&gt;! (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3783483815&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8774&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8774/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8774&quot;&gt;#8774&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Git apply path parsing now handles quoted/escaped paths and &lt;code&gt;/dev/null&lt;/code&gt; correctly to avoid misclassified changes. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3788571692&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8824&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8824/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8824&quot;&gt;#8824&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;

&lt;ul&gt;

&lt;/ul&gt;</content:encoded></item><item><title>Codex CLI Release: 0.78.0</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-274610568</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-274610568</guid><description>0.78.0</description><pubDate>Tue, 06 Jan 2026 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded>&lt;h2&gt;New Features&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Add &lt;code&gt;Ctrl+G&lt;/code&gt; to open the current prompt in your configured external editor (&lt;code&gt;$VISUAL&lt;/code&gt;/&lt;code&gt;$EDITOR&lt;/code&gt;) and sync edits back into the TUI. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3696482899&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/7606&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/7606/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/7606&quot;&gt;#7606&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Support project-aware config layering: load repo-local &lt;code&gt;.codex/config.toml&lt;/code&gt;, honor configurable &lt;code&gt;project_root_markers&lt;/code&gt;, and merge that with system config like &lt;code&gt;/etc/codex/config.toml&lt;/code&gt;. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3749525389&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8354&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8354/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8354&quot;&gt;#8354&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3749728592&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8359&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8359/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8359&quot;&gt;#8359&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3755717046&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8461&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8461/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8461&quot;&gt;#8461&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Support enterprise-managed configuration requirements on macOS via an MDM-provided TOML payload. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3781879209&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8743&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8743/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8743&quot;&gt;#8743&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Improve &lt;code&gt;tui2&lt;/code&gt; transcript navigation with multi-click selection, a copy shortcut/affordance, and a draggable auto-hiding scrollbar. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3755725901&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8462&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8462/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8462&quot;&gt;#8462&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3756429960&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8471&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8471/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8471&quot;&gt;#8471&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3780153990&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8728&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8728/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8728&quot;&gt;#8728&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Start Windows PowerShell sessions in UTF-8 mode to reduce encoding-related prompt/output issues. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3721433888&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/7902&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/7902/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/7902&quot;&gt;#7902&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Exec policy rules can now include human-readable justifications, and policy loading follows the unified config-layer stack. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3749318209&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8349&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8349/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8349&quot;&gt;#8349&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3755501763&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8453&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8453/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8453&quot;&gt;#8453&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3782611905&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8751&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8751/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8751&quot;&gt;#8751&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Bug Fixes&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Fix failures when the model returns multiple tool calls in a single turn by emitting tool calls in the format the Chat Completions API expects. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3763623336&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8556&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8556/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8556&quot;&gt;#8556&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Make &lt;code&gt;/review&lt;/code&gt; compute diffs from the session’s working directory so base-branch detection works correctly with runtime cwd overrides. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3781229801&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8738&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8738/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8738&quot;&gt;#8738&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Handle the legacy Chat Completions streaming terminator cleanly to avoid spurious SSE parse errors. (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3778475470&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8708&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8708/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8708&quot;&gt;#8708&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Fix a set of &lt;code&gt;tui2&lt;/code&gt; rendering/input edge cases (screen corruption, scroll stickiness, and selection/copy correctness). (&lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3755789126&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8463&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8463/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8463&quot;&gt;#8463&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3777628965&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8695&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8695/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8695&quot;&gt;#8695&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a class=&quot;issue-link js-issue-link&quot; data-error-text=&quot;Failed to load title&quot; data-id=&quot;3755364798&quot; data-permission-text=&quot;Title is private&quot; data-url=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/issues/8449&quot; data-hovercard-type=&quot;pull_request&quot; data-hovercard-url=&quot;/openai/codex/pull/8449/hovercard&quot; href=&quot;https://github.com/openai/codex/pull/8449&quot;&gt;#8449&lt;/a&gt;)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Improve diagnostics when &lt;code&gt;ripgrep&lt;/code&gt; download fails during CLI packaging so failures are easier to debug. &lt;/ul&gt;</content:encoded></item><item><title>Agent skills in Codex</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-12-19-mdx</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-12-19-mdx</guid><description>Agent skills in Codex</description><pubDate>Fri, 19 Dec 2025 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded># Agent skills in Codex

Codex now supports **agent skills**: reusable bundles of instructions (plus optional scripts and resources) that help Codex reliably complete specific tasks.

Skills are available in both the Codex CLI and IDE extensions.

You can invoke a skill explicitly by typing `$skill-name` (for example, `$skill-installer` or the experimental `$create-plan` skill after installing it), or let Codex select a skill automatically based on your prompt.

Learn more in the [skills documentation](/codex/skills).

#### Folder-based standard (agentskills.io)

Following the open [agent skills specification](https://agentskills.io/specification), a skill is a folder with a required `SKILL.md` and optional supporting files:

```text
my-skill/
  SKILL.md       # Required: instructions + metadata
  scripts/       # Optional: executable code
  references/    # Optional: documentation
  assets/        # Optional: templates, resources
```

#### Install skills per-user or per-repo

You can install skills for just yourself in `~/.codex/skills`, or for everyone on a project by checking them into `.codex/skills` in the repository.

Codex also ships with a few built-in system skills to get started, including `$skill-creator` and `$skill-installer`. The `$create-plan` skill is experimental and needs to be installed (for example: `$skill-installer install the create-plan skill from the .experimental folder`).

#### Curated skills directory

Codex ships with a [small curated set of skills](https://github.com/openai/skills) inspired by popular workflows at OpenAI. Install them with `$skill-installer`, and expect more over time.</content:encoded></item><item><title>Codex CLI Release: 0.76.0</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-271840565</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-271840565</guid><description>0.76.0</description><pubDate>Fri, 19 Dec 2025 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded>&lt;h3&gt;New Features&lt;/h3&gt;

&lt;/ul&gt;</content:encoded></item><item><title>Introducing GPT-5.2-Codex</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-12-18-mdx</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-12-18-mdx</guid><description>Introducing GPT-5.2-Codex</description><pubDate>Thu, 18 Dec 2025 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded># Introducing GPT-5.2-Codex

[Today we are releasing GPT-5.2-Codex](http://www.openai.com/index/gpt-5-2-codex), the most advanced agentic coding model yet for complex, real-world software engineering.

GPT-5.2-Codex is a version of [GPT-5.2](https://openai.com/index/introducing-gpt-5-2/) further optimized for agentic coding in Codex, including improvements on long-horizon work through context compaction, stronger performance on large code changes like refactors and migrations, improved performance in Windows environments, and significantly stronger cybersecurity capabilities.

Starting today, the CLI and IDE Extension will default to `gpt-5.2-codex` for users who are signed in with ChatGPT. API access for the model will come soon.

If you have a model specified in your [`config.toml` configuration file](/codex/local-config), you can instead try out `gpt-5.2-codex` for a new Codex CLI session using:

```bash
codex --model gpt-5.2-codex
```

You can also use the `/model` slash command in the CLI. In the Codex IDE Extension you can select GPT-5.2-Codex from the dropdown menu.

If you want to switch for all sessions, you can change your default model to `gpt-5.2-codex` by updating your `config.toml` [configuration file](/codex/local-config):

```toml
model = &quot;gpt-5.2-codex”
```</content:encoded></item><item><title>Codex CLI Release: 0.75.0</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-271555285</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#github-release-271555285</guid><description>0.75.0</description><pubDate>Thu, 18 Dec 2025 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded>&lt;h3&gt;PRs Merged&lt;/h3&gt;

Assign or mention @Codex in an issue to kick-off a Codex cloud task. As Codex works, it posts updates back to Linear, providing a link to the completed task so you can review, open a PR, or keep working.

![Screenshot of a successful Codex task started in Linear](/images/codex/integrations/linear-codex-example.png)

To learn more about how to connect Codex to Linear both locally through MCP and through the new integration, check out the [Codex for Linear documentation](/codex/integrations/linear).</content:encoded></item><item><title>Usage and credits fixes</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-11-24-mdx</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-11-24-mdx</guid><description>Usage and credits fixes</description><pubDate>Mon, 24 Nov 2025 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded># Usage and credits fixes

Minor updates to address a few issues with Codex usage and credits:

- Adjusted all usage dashboards to show &quot;limits remaining&quot; for consistency. The CLI previously displayed &quot;limits used.&quot;
- Fixed an issue preventing users from buying credits if their ChatGPT subscription was purchased via iOS or Google Play.
- Fixed an issue where the CLI could display stale usage information; it now refreshes without needing to send a message first.
- Optimized the backend to help smooth out usage throughout the day, irrespective of overall Codex load or how traffic is routed. Before, users could get unlucky and hit a few cache misses in a row, leading to much less usage.</content:encoded></item><item><title>Introducing GPT-5.1-Codex-Max</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-11-18-mdx</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-11-18-mdx</guid><description>Introducing GPT-5.1-Codex-Max</description><pubDate>Tue, 18 Nov 2025 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded># Introducing GPT-5.1-Codex-Max

[Today we are releasing GPT-5.1-Codex-Max](http://www.openai.com/index/gpt-5-1-codex-max), our new frontier agentic coding model.

GPT‑5.1-Codex-Max is built on an update to our foundational reasoning model, which is trained on agentic tasks across software engineering, math, research, and more. GPT‑5.1-Codex-Max is faster, more intelligent, and more token-efficient at every stage of the development cycle–and a new step towards becoming a reliable coding partner.

Starting today, the CLI and IDE Extension will default to `gpt-5.1-codex-max` for users that are signed in with ChatGPT. API access for the model will come soon.

For non-latency-sensitive tasks, we’ve also added a new Extra High (`xhigh`) reasoning effort, which lets the model think for an even longer period of time for a better answer. We still recommend medium as your daily driver for most tasks.

If you have a model specified in your [`config.toml` configuration file](/codex/local-config), you can instead try out `gpt-5.1-codex-max` for a new Codex CLI session using:

```bash
codex --model gpt-5.1-codex-max
```

You can also use the `/model` slash command in the CLI. In the Codex IDE Extension you can select GPT-5.1-Codex from the dropdown menu.

If you want to switch for all sessions, you can change your default model to `gpt-5.1-codex-max` by updating your `config.toml` [configuration file](/codex/local-config):

```toml
model = &quot;gpt-5.1-codex-max”
```</content:encoded></item><item><title>Introducing GPT-5.1-Codex and GPT-5.1-Codex-Mini</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-11-13-mdx</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-11-13-mdx</guid><description>Introducing GPT-5.1-Codex and GPT-5.1-Codex-Mini</description><pubDate>Thu, 13 Nov 2025 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded># Introducing GPT-5.1-Codex and GPT-5.1-Codex-Mini

Along with the [GPT-5.1 launch in the API](https://openai.com/index/gpt-5-1-for-developers/), we are introducing new `gpt-5.1-codex-mini` and `gpt-5.1-codex` model options in Codex, a version of GPT-5.1 optimized for long-running, agentic coding tasks and use in coding agent harnesses in Codex or Codex-like harnesses.

Starting today, the CLI and IDE Extension will default to `gpt-5.1-codex` on macOS and Linux and `gpt-5.1` on Windows.

If you have a model specified in your [`config.toml` configuration file](/codex/local-config), you can instead try out `gpt-5.1-codex` for a new Codex CLI session using:

```bash
codex --model gpt-5.1-codex
```

You can also use the `/model` slash command in the CLI. In the Codex IDE Extension you can select GPT-5.1-Codex from the dropdown menu.

If you want to switch for all sessions, you can change your default model to `gpt-5.1-codex` by updating your `config.toml` [configuration file](/codex/local-config):

```toml
model = &quot;gpt-5.1-codex”
```</content:encoded></item><item><title>Introducing GPT-5-Codex-Mini</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-11-07-mdx</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-11-07-mdx</guid><description>Introducing GPT-5-Codex-Mini</description><pubDate>Fri, 07 Nov 2025 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded># Introducing GPT-5-Codex-Mini

Today we are introducing a new `gpt-5-codex-mini` model option to Codex CLI and the IDE Extension. The model is a smaller, more cost-effective, but less capable version of `gpt-5-codex` that provides approximately 4x more usage as part of your ChatGPT subscription.

Starting today, the CLI and IDE Extension will automatically suggest switching to `gpt-5-codex-mini` when you reach 90% of your 5-hour usage limit, to help you work longer without interruptions.

You can try the model for a new Codex CLI session using:

```bash
codex --model gpt-5-codex-mini
```

You can also use the `/model` slash command in the CLI. In the Codex IDE Extension you can select GPT-5-Codex-Mini from the dropdown menu.

Alternatively, you can change your default model to `gpt-5-codex-mini` by updating your `config.toml` [configuration file](/codex/local-config):

```toml
model = &quot;gpt-5-codex-mini”
```</content:encoded></item><item><title>GPT-5-Codex model update</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-11-06-mdx</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-11-06-mdx</guid><description>GPT-5-Codex model update</description><pubDate>Thu, 06 Nov 2025 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded># GPT-5-Codex model update

You can now tag `@codex` on a teammate&apos;s pull request to ask clarifying questions, request a follow-up, or ask Codex to make changes. GitHub Issues now also support `@codex` mentions, so you can kick off tasks from any issue, without leaving your workflow.

![Codex responding to a GitHub pull request and issue after an @Codex mention.](/images/codex/integrations/github-example.png)</content:encoded></item><item><title>Codex is now GA</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-10-06-mdx</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-10-06-mdx</guid><description>Codex is now GA</description><pubDate>Mon, 06 Oct 2025 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded># Codex is now GA

Codex is now generally available with 3 new features — @Codex in Slack, Codex SDK, and new admin tools.

#### @Codex in Slack

![](/images/codex/integrations/slack-example.png)

You can now questions and assign tasks to Codex directly from Slack. See the [Slack guide](/codex/integrations/slack) to get started.

#### Codex SDK

Integrate the same agent that powers the Codex CLI inside your own tools and workflows with the Codex SDK in Typescript. With the new Codex GitHub Action, you can easily add Codex to CI/CD workflows. See the [Codex SDK guide](/codex/sdk) to get started.

```ts


const agent = new Codex();
const thread = await agent.startThread();

const result = await thread.run(&quot;Explore this repo&quot;);
console.log(result);

const result2 = await thread.run(&quot;Propose changes&quot;);
console.log(result2);
```

#### New admin controls and analytics

![](/images/codex/enterprise/analytics.png)

ChatGPT workspace admins can now edit or delete Codex Cloud environments. With managed config files, they can set safe defaults for CLI and IDE usage and monitor how Codex uses commands locally. New analytics dashboards help you track Codex usage and code review feedback. Learn more in the [enterprise admin guide.](/codex/enterprise/admin-setup)

#### Availability and pricing updates

The Slack integration and Codex SDK are available to developers on ChatGPT Plus, Pro, Business, Edu, and Enterprise plans starting today, while the new admin features will be available to Business, Edu, and Enterprise.
Beginning October 20, Codex Cloud tasks will count toward your Codex usage. Review the [Codex pricing guide](/codex/pricing) for plan-specific details.</content:encoded></item><item><title>GPT-5-Codex in the API</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-09-23-mdx</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-09-23-mdx</guid><description>GPT-5-Codex in the API</description><pubDate>Tue, 23 Sep 2025 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded># GPT-5-Codex in the API

#### New model: GPT-5-Codex

![codex-switch-model](https://cdn.openai.com/devhub/docs/codex-switch-model.png)

GPT-5-Codex is a version of GPT-5 further optimized for agentic coding in Codex.
It&apos;s available in the IDE extension and CLI when you sign in with your ChatGPT account.
It also powers the cloud agent and Code Review in GitHub.

To learn more about GPT-5-Codex and how it performs compared to GPT-5 on software engineering tasks, see our [announcement blog post](https://openai.com/index/introducing-upgrades-to-codex/).

#### Image outputs

![codex-image-outputs](https://cdn.openai.com/devhub/docs/codex-image-output.png)

When working in the cloud on front-end engineering tasks, GPT-5-Codex can now display screenshots of the UI in Codex web for you to review. With image output, you can iterate on the design without needing to check out the branch locally.

#### New in Codex CLI

- You can now resume sessions where you left off with `codex resume`.
- Context compaction automatically summarizes the session as it approaches the context window limit.

Learn more in the [latest release notes](https://github.com/openai/codex/releases/tag/rust-v0.36.0)</content:encoded></item><item><title>Late August update</title><link>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-08-27-mdx</link><guid>https://developers.openai.com/changelog/#codex-2025-08-27-mdx</guid><description>Late August update</description><pubDate>Wed, 27 Aug 2025 00:00:00 GMT</pubDate><content:encoded># Late August update

#### Image inputs

![](/images/codex/changelog/image_input.png)

You can now attach images to your prompts in Codex web. This is great for asking Codex to implement frontend changes or follow up on whiteboarding sessions.

#### Container caching

![](/images/codex/changelog/container_caching.png)

Codex now caches containers to start new tasks and followups 90% faster, dropping the median start time from 48 seconds to 5 seconds. You can optionally configure a maintenance script to update the environment from its cached state to prepare for new tasks. See the docs for more.

#### Automatic environment setup

Now, environments without manual setup scripts automatically run the standard installation commands for common package managers like yarn, pnpm, npm, go mod, gradle, pip, poetry, uv, and cargo. #### Agent internet access

![](/images/codex/changelog/internet_access.png)

Now you can give Codex access to the internet during task execution to install dependencies, upgrade packages, run tests that need external resources, and more.

Internet access is off by default. Plus, Pro, and Business users can enable it for specific environments, with granular control of which domains and HTTP methods Codex can access. Internet access for Enterprise users is coming soon.

Learn more about usage and risks in the [docs](/codex/cloud/agent-internet).

#### Update existing PRs

![](/images/codex/changelog/update_prs.png)

Now you can update existing pull requests when following up on a task.

#### Voice dictation

![](/images/codex/changelog/voice_dictation.gif)

Now you can dictate tasks to Codex.
